        <![CDATA[<p>A brand new fiction podcast from Night Vale Presents: <em><a href="http://www.nightvalepresents.com/dreamboy" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">Dreamboy</a></em>. Dane, a spun-out musician spending the winter in Cleveland, Ohio, has two main goals: keeping his job at the Pepper Heights Zoo and trying not to waste all his time on Grindr. What he doesn’t expect is to get swept into a story about dreams, about forevers, about flickering lights, about unexplained deaths, about relentless change, and about the parts of ourselves that we wish other people knew to look for. Oh, and also a murderous zebra.<br>

    <item>
      <guid isPermaLink="false">prx_126_6f122cc4-1379-4cde-a3be-7fbe88dd4f3f</guid>
      <title>Adventures in New America: Episode One, The End</title>
      <pubDate>Wed, 03 Oct 2018 04:00:00 -0000</pubDate>
      <link>https://beta.prx.org/stories/255663</link>
      <description>
        <![CDATA[<p>A brand new fiction podcast from Night Vale Presents: ADVENTURES IN NEW AMERICA, the first sci-fi, political satire, Afrofuturistic buddy comedy, serialized for New Americans in a new and desperate time.<br>
<br>
To keep listening to Adventures in New America, find it on <a href="https://itunes.apple.com/us/podcast/adventures-in-new-america/id1434863731?mt=2" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">Apple Podcasts</a> or <a href="http://www.nightvalepresents.com/adventuresinnewamerica" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">wherever you listen to podcasts</a>.</p>

<p>New American citizens are terrorized by supernatural beings. A man with cancer who has given up on life is saved by a younger sociopathic girl he meets outside of a poke bowl restaurant. Somebody’s baby is crying: is it yours?</p>

    <item>
      <guid isPermaLink="false">prx_126_9bf30773-38cf-43be-8979-0cbc8fd95702</guid>
      <title>The Summer of Night Vale Presents, Part 4</title>
      <pubDate>Fri, 27 Jul 2018 04:00:00 -0000</pubDate>
      <link>https://beta.prx.org/stories/250062</link>
      <description>
        <![CDATA[<p>Welcome to the fourth and final week of the Summer of Night Vale Presents, a celebration and sampling of some of the shows across our network. This week, hear previews of two upcoming Night Vale Presents shows, and full episodes from <a href="https://www.wnycstudios.org/shows/orbitinghumancircus" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">The Orbiting Human Circus (of the Air)</a> and <a href="http://goodmorningnightvale.com" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">Good Morning Night Vale</a>.</p>

<p>To get updates on our new shows, Adventures in New America and Dreamboy, sign up for the <a href="http://eepurl.com/b19UIv" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">Night Vale Presents newsletter</a>, or follow us on <a href="https://www.facebook.com/nightvalepresents/" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">Facebook</a> and <a href="http://twitter.com/nvpresents" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">Twitter</a>.</p>

<p><a href="https://www.wnycstudios.org/shows/orbitinghumancircus" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">The Orbiting Human Circus (of the Air)</a> is a surreal and funny audio drama about a lonely janitor at the Eiffel Tower who longs to be part of the most popular radio show in the world. Recently, we re-issued the first season in partnership with WNYC. This special edition has brand new behind-the-scenes commentary in every episode and a director’s cut of the season finale, and is the perfect excuse to either re-listen or dive in for the very first time.</p>

<p><a href="http://goodmorningnightvale.com" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">Good Morning Night Vale</a> is the official Welcome to Night Vale recap show, hosted by cast members Meg Bashwiner, Symphony Sanders, and Hal Lublin. Each week, our hosts do a deep dive into one episode of Welcome to Night Vale, starting with the very first episode from 2012. Tune in for behind-the-scenes stories, interviews with the cast and creators, fan theories, and THROAT SPIDERS.</p>]]>

      <title>The Summer of Night Vale Presents, Part 2</title>

        <![CDATA[<p>This is the Summer of Night Vale Presents, a celebration and sampling of some of the shows across our network. This week, we hear from two of our newest fiction shows, <a href="http://poundedinthebuttbymyownpodcast.com" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">Pounded In The Butt By My Own Podcast</a> and <a href="http://itmakesasound.com" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">It Makes A Sound</a>. Plus, an update on <a href="http://withinthewires.com" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">Within the Wires</a> Season 3.</p>

<p><a href="http://withinthewires.com" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">Within the Wires</a> returns on September 4. Each season tells a new story in the same world, using a single set of found audio. Season One is a prison break / romance told entirely through relaxation tapes. Season Two is the mystery of a missing woman told through a decade’s worth of museum audio guides. Season Three, coming this September, is a political thriller told through dictaphone recordings to a secretary.</p>

<p><a href="http://poundedinthebuttbymyownpodcast.com" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">Pounded In The Butt By My Own Podcast</a> is our collaboration with celebrated author Chuck Tingle. Chuck’s short stories have entertained and aroused readers across the world, and we are excited to bring his stories to life with performances by celebrity guests like Cecil Baldwin, Mara Wilson, and Becca Blackwell. Whether you’re new to the Tingleverse or have lived there for years, this is the podcast about love that you never knew you needed.<br>
<br>
<a href="http://itmakesasound.com" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">It Makes A Sound</a> is the story of a woman named Deirdre who finds a cassette tape from 1992 in her attic. What follows is a surprising story about family, memory, and music that goes places that you don’t expect. Join her quest to make Rosemary Hills come back to life with the sound of music.</p>

<p>Find out more about these shows, and all of the shows on our network, by visiting <a href="http://nightvalepresents.com/" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">nightvalepresents.com.</a></p>]]>

      <guid isPermaLink="false">prx_126_6761728f-414c-4d8b-bf99-10a78b99137d</guid>
      <title>The Summer of Night Vale Presents, Part 1</title>
      <pubDate>Fri, 06 Jul 2018 04:00:00 -0000</pubDate>
      <link>https://beta.prx.org/stories/248217</link>
      <description>
        <![CDATA[<p>Welcome to the Summer of Night Vale Presents, a celebration and sampling of some of the shows across our network. This week: a look at two of our non-fiction shows, <a href="http://ionlylistentothemountaingoats.com" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">I Only Listen to the Mountain Goats</a> and <a href="http://conversationswithpeoplewhohateme.com" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">Conversations with People Who Hate Me</a>.</p>

<p><a href="http://ionlylistentothemountaingoats.com" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">I Only Listen to the Mountain Goats</a> is a show about what it means to be an artist, to be a fan, and as many people are, both at once. Our first season found Welcome to Night Vale creator Joseph Fink in conversation with John Darnielle, singer and songwriter of the Mountain Goats, about their album <em>All Hail West Texas</em>. You’ll hear an excerpt from episode 9, “The Mess Inside,” which shows how these conversations wander through topics in unexpected ways.<br>
<br>
<a href="http://conversationswithpeoplewhohateme.com" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">Conversations with People Who Hate Me</a> is a show where Dylan Marron, whom you may know as Carlos the Scientist on Welcome to Night Vale, takes contentious online conversations and moves them offline. This year, Dylan has been moderating conversations between people who have exchanged their own online negativity. You’ll hear the entirety of episode 12, “Burned at the Stake,” featuring a woman who wrote about why the TV show <em>The Office</em> doesn’t hold up to today’s standards and a man who told her she should be burned at the stake.</p>

<p>Find out more about these shows, and all of the shows on our network, by visiting <a href="http://nightvalepresents.com" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">nightvalepresents.com.</a></p>]]>

    <item>
      <guid isPermaLink="false">prx_126_143bc520-c7d2-4242-bc4e-7799ccf997db</guid>
      <title>130 - A Story About Us</title>
      <pubDate>Fri, 15 Jun 2018 04:00:00 -0000</pubDate>
      <link>https://beta.prx.org/stories/246224</link>
      <description>
        <![CDATA[<p>This is a story about us, said the man on the radio, and we were pleased, because we always wanted to hear about ourselves on the radio.</p>

<p>Weather: “Space and Time” by Joseph Fink<br>
<a href="https://josephfink.bandcamp.com" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">https://josephfink.bandcamp.com</a></p>

<p>Just announced: Welcome to Night Vale World Tour 2018 / 2019. Our brand new live show is coming to over 40 cities across North America, the UK, and Europe. Tickets on sale June 22, member pre-sale June 20.<br>
<a href="http://www.welcometonightvale.com/live" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">http://www.welcometonightvale.com/live</a></p>

<p>Music: Disparition<br>
<a href="http://disparition.info/" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">http://disparition.info</a></p>

<p>Logo: Rob Wilson<br>

        <![CDATA[<p>We’re checking back in with our most recent episode of I Only Listen to the Mountain Goats to share with you what the show has become. Thanks for listening!<br>
<br>
“Jeff Davis County Blues” is a song with a particular meaning to Joseph's life. Julian Koster of The Music Tapes and The Orbiting Human Circus (of the Air) joins to share his dream-inspired cover.</p>

<p>Buy Julian Koster’s cover of “Jeff Davis County Blues” on iTunes, <strong><a href="https://themountaingoats.bandcamp.com/album/i-only-listen-to-the-mountain-goats" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">Bandcamp</a></strong>, or wherever you buy digital music. It supports both the artist and the show!</p>

<p><strong><a href="https://www.mergerecords.com/i-only-listen-to-the-mountain-goats-ahwt" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">Pre-order the full cover album on vinyl</a></strong>.<br>
<br>
I Only Listen to the Mountain Goats t-shirts and tote bags <strong><a href="https://topatoco.com/collections/iolttmg" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">now available</a></strong>.</p>

<p>Learn more about John Darnielle’s two novels <strong><a href="http://www.johndarnielle.com/" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">here</a></strong>.<br>
Listen to more music by the Mountain Goats, including their latest album <em>Goths</em>, <strong><a href="http://www.mountain-goats.com/" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">here</a></strong>.</p>

<p>Check out Joseph Fink’s other shows, <strong><a href="http://www.welcometonightvale.com/" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">Welcome to Night Vale</a></strong> and <strong><a href="http://aliceisntdead.com/" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">Alice Isn’t Dead</a></strong>. His second novel with Jeffrey Cranor, <strong><em><a href="http://www.welcometonightvale.com/books/" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">It Devours!</a></em></strong>, is out now.</p>

<p>Thanks to our sponsor Lincoln in the Bardo, published by Random House and available wherever books are sold! This episode was also sponsored by Bombfell, an easier way for men to get better clothes. Get 25% off your first order at <strong><a href="https://www.bombfell.com/goats" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">bombfell.com/goats</a></strong>.</p>

        <![CDATA[<p>Part 1 of 3: A case of Canadian Club has been hidden in Night Vale.</p>

<p>This episode was co-written with Glen David Gold.</p>

<p>The voice of Hugh Jackman was Hunter Canning.</p>

<p>The voice of Missy Wilks was Lusia Strus.</p>

      <title>New Podcast Teaser: CONVERSATIONS WITH PEOPLE WHO HATE ME</title>
      <pubDate>Tue, 11 Jul 2017 19:06:14 -0000</pubDate>
      <link>https://beta.prx.org/stories/229605</link>
      <description>
        <![CDATA[<p>A brand new podcast from Dylan Marron (the voice of Carlos the Scientist) and Night Vale Presents: Conversations with People Who Hate Me. </p>

<p>Conversations with People Who Hate Me takes hateful conversations online and turns them into productive conversations offline. As a writer and video maker who focuses on social justice issues, Dylan Marron receives a lot of negative messages on the internet. In this new podcast he calls some of the folks who wrote them to ask one simple question: why? What follows is a complicated and sometimes hilarious navigation of two strangers getting to know each other.</p>

<p>Season 1 premieres on July 31, with new episodes released weekly.</p>

<p>Produced by Night Vale Presents, the people who brought you Welcome to Night Vale, Alice Isn't Dead, Within the Wires, and The Orbiting Human Circus (of the Air).</p>
